<script>
    // 关闭补看弹窗
    $(".btn_close").on("click",function(){
        $(".tan-catalog").hide()
    })

    // 补看点击事件
    $(".repar_view").on("click",function(){
        var videoId = $(this).data("video-id").toString();
        var backStatus = $(this).data("back-id");
        var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoId,backStatus);
    })

    // 获取补看数据
    function getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoID,backStatus){
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+"/video/videoPlay/getVideoCatchInfo.shtm",
            {
                cwareID:cwareID,
                videoID:videoID,
                r:Math.random()
            },
            function(data){
                var videoRefID = "&#39;" + "1.1." + cwareID + "." + videoID + "&#39;";
                var timeMap;
                if(data){
                    timeMap = data;
                }else{
                    timeMap = JSON.parse(pageData.catchTimeMap);
                }
                var timeStr = timeMap[videoID];
                if(timeStr){
                    var timeArray = timeStr.split(",");
                    // 清空原来的内容
                    $(".tan-catalog-con ul").empty();
                    // 根据数组动态生成
                    timeArray.forEach(function (time) {
                        var startTime = time.split("-")[0];
                        var endTime = time.split("-")[1];
                        var li = "<li>";
                        li += "<span class='flV2'>" + time + "</span>"
                        li += "<em class='fr' onclick='playVideoByRefId(" + videoRefID +  ',' + "&#39;" + startTime + "&#39;" + ',' + backStatus + ',' + "&#39;" + endTime + "&#39;" + ")'></em>";
                        li += "</li>";
                        $(".tan-catalog-con ul").append(li);
                    });
                }
                // 显示弹窗
                $(".tan-catalog").show();
            }
        );
    }

    // 播放器跳转方法
    function playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime){
        cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime);
    }

	//20220505 add 提示
	var testLeftRoll = function(id,rollId){
		if($(id).length && $(id).length>0){
			var _id = $(id),
				_roll = _id.find(rollId),
				id_w = _id.width(),
				roll_w = _roll.width();
			if(roll_w > id_w){
				_roll.append(_roll.find('p').clone()).width(roll_w*2)
				var num = 0,
				goLeft = function() {
					if (num == '-' + roll_w){
						num = 0;
					}
					num -= 1;
					_roll.css({
						left: num
					})
				}
				//设置滚动速度
				var timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				//设置鼠标经过时滚动停止
				_id.hover(function() {
					clearInterval(timer);
				},
				function() {
					timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				})
			}
		}
	}
	setTimeout(function (){
		testLeftRoll('.clc-announcement-main','.clc-announcement-roll');
	},2000);

	//打开课件更新题型
	$('.viewBtn').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').show();
	})
	$('.updatePromptBox .close-box').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').hide();
	})

<script>
	var showPointTest = function (pointVideoLen, pointOpenType) {
		window.testController.showPoint4Click(pointVideoLen, pointOpenType);
	}

	var closeTest = function () {
	}

	var csPop = function (el,nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID) {
		var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
		var videoID = pageData.videoID;
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+'/testPop/getPointFlag.shtm',{
            cwareID:cwareID,
            videoID:videoID,
            r:Math.random()
        },function(data){
			// 控制div显示（0 都不显示设置选项，1 都显示显示，2 显示知识点测试，3 显示单元测试）
			var test = data[0];
			console.log(test);
			// 两个设置选项
			var setPointTest = $('#setPointTest');
			var setUnitTest = $('#setUnitTest');
			switch (test.settingFlag) {
				case 1:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				case 2:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
				case 3:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				default:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
			}
            $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
            $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
			$("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");

            for (var i = 0, len = data.length; i < len; i++) {
                var test = data[i];
                var currOpenType = test.pointOpenType;
                switch (currOpenType) {
                    case "z": //知识点测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"zPopFlag0":"zPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
                    case "d": //单元测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"dPopFlag0":"dPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
					case "t": //知识点练习
						var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"tPopFlag0":"tPopFlag1"
						$("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
						break;
                    default :
                        $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        break;
                }
            }

        });
		var _this = $("." + el);
		var myHeight = _this.height();
		_this.css("marginTop", -myHeight / 2)
		$(".mask").show();
		_this.show();
	}

<script>
    // 关闭补看弹窗
    $(".btn_close").on("click",function(){
        $(".tan-catalog").hide()
    })

    // 补看点击事件
    $(".repar_view").on("click",function(){
        var videoId = $(this).data("video-id").toString();
        var backStatus = $(this).data("back-id");
        var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoId,backStatus);
    })

    // 获取补看数据
    function getVideoCatchInfo(cwareID,videoID,backStatus){
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+"/video/videoPlay/getVideoCatchInfo.shtm",
            {
                cwareID:cwareID,
                videoID:videoID,
                r:Math.random()
            },
            function(data){
                var videoRefID = "&#39;" + "1.1." + cwareID + "." + videoID + "&#39;";
                var timeMap;
                if(data){
                    timeMap = data;
                }else{
                    timeMap = JSON.parse(pageData.catchTimeMap);
                }
                var timeStr = timeMap[videoID];
                if(timeStr){
                    var timeArray = timeStr.split(",");
                    // 清空原来的内容
                    $(".tan-catalog-con ul").empty();
                    // 根据数组动态生成
                    timeArray.forEach(function (time) {
                        var startTime = time.split("-")[0];
                        var endTime = time.split("-")[1];
                        var li = "<li>";
                        li += "<span class='flV2'>" + time + "</span>"
                        li += "<em class='fr' onclick='playVideoByRefId(" + videoRefID +  ',' + "&#39;" + startTime + "&#39;" + ',' + backStatus + ',' + "&#39;" + endTime + "&#39;" + ")'></em>";
                        li += "</li>";
                        $(".tan-catalog-con ul").append(li);
                    });
                }
                // 显示弹窗
                $(".tan-catalog").show();
            }
        );
    }

    // 播放器跳转方法
    function playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime){
        cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideoByRefId(videoRefId,startTime,backStatus,endTime);
    }

	//20220505 add 提示
	var testLeftRoll = function(id,rollId){
		if($(id).length && $(id).length>0){
			var _id = $(id),
				_roll = _id.find(rollId),
				id_w = _id.width(),
				roll_w = _roll.width();
			if(roll_w > id_w){
				_roll.append(_roll.find('p').clone()).width(roll_w*2)
				var num = 0,
				goLeft = function() {
					if (num == '-' + roll_w){
						num = 0;
					}
					num -= 1;
					_roll.css({
						left: num
					})
				}
				//设置滚动速度
				var timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				//设置鼠标经过时滚动停止
				_id.hover(function() {
					clearInterval(timer);
				},
				function() {
					timer = setInterval(goLeft, 40);
				})
			}
		}
	}
	setTimeout(function (){
		testLeftRoll('.clc-announcement-main','.clc-announcement-roll');
	},2000);

	//打开课件更新题型
	$('.viewBtn').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').show();
	})
	$('.updatePromptBox .close-box').click(function(){
		$('.updatePromptBox,.updateMask').hide();
	})
</script>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>1.下列关于收入确认时间的说法，不符合企业所得税相关规定的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.广告的制作费根据制作广告的完工进度确认<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.利息收入按债权人实际收到利息的日期确认<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.接受捐赠收入按实际收到捐赠资产的日期确认<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.特许权使用费收入按照合同约定的特许权使用人应付特许权使用费的日期确认<br>

『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』应确认企业所得税应纳税所得额＝4 000×50＝200 000（元）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>『提示』销售商品以旧换新的，销售商品应当按照销售商品收入确认条件确认收入，回收的商品作为购进商品处理。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>3.我国境内企业甲公司接受外国关联企业乙公司一笔混合性投资并向其分配投资收益。乙公司按本国税法规定将其认定为权益性投资收益且享受免税待遇。下列对甲公司支付投资收益的企业所得税处理，符合税法规定的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.免征预提所得税<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.不征预提所得税<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.应视为股息分配<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.应视为利息支出<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255827_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255827_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255827_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255827_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255827_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255827_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255827_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255827_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』境外投资者在境内从事混合性投资业务，同时符合以下两种情形的，境内被投资企业向境外投资者支付的利息应视为股息，不得进行税前扣除：①该境外投资者与境内被投资企业构成关联关系；②境外投资者所在国家（地区）将该项投资收益认定为权益性投资收益，且不征收企业所得税。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>4.2024年7月，甲公司投资于境内非上市乙公司，其股权的计税基础为1 000万元，持有的股权比例为20％。2024年8月，乙公司将股权溢价发行形成的资本公积800万元转增股本。2024年11月甲公司转让该股权取得收入1 500万元。甲公司股权转让所得为（　）万元。<br>

『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』被投资企业将股权（票）溢价所形成的资本公积转为股本的，不作为投资方企业的股息、红利收入，投资方企业也不得增加该项长期投资的计税基础。股权转让所得＝1 500－1 000＝500（万元）。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>5.企业持有的下列资产中，所计提的折旧准予在企业所得税税前扣除的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.未投入使用的办公楼<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.已足额提取折旧仍继续使用的固定资产<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.以经营租赁方式租入的汽车<br>

『正确答案』A<br>
『答案解析』选项B，企业购买的文物、艺术品用于收藏、展示、保值增值的，作为投资资产进行税务处理。文物、艺术品资产在持有期间，计提的折旧、摊销费用，不得税前扣除。选项C、D，下列固定资产不得计算折旧扣除：房屋、建筑物以外未投入使用的固定资产；以经营租赁方式租入的固定资产；以融资租赁方式租出的固定资产；已足额提取折旧仍继续使用的固定资产；与经营活动无关的固定资产；单独估价作为固定资产入账的土地；其他不得计算折旧扣除的固定资产。<br>

『正确答案』B<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>『提示』适用特殊性税务处理时，重组交易各方对交易中股权支付暂不确认有关资产的转让所得或损失的，其非股权支付仍应当在交易当期确认相应资产的所得或损失，并调整相应资产的计税基础。非股权支付对应的资产转让所得或损失＝（被转让资产的公允价值－被转让资产的计税基础）×（非股权支付金额÷被转让资产的公允价值）。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>11.2023年11月甲企业购进符合税法规定可享受税额抵免优惠政策安全生产专用设备一台，增值税专用发票注明金额100万元、税额13万元。甲企业已申报抵扣进项税额,并享受了企业所得税抵免优惠。2024年11月甲企业将该设备转让给乙企业，下列税务处理正确的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.乙企业不得享受企业所得税抵免优惠<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.甲企业转让设备可税前扣除的资产净值为113万元<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.甲企业转让设备时应转出已抵扣的进项税额<br>

『正确答案』B<br>
『答案解析』选项A，享受税额抵免企业所得税优惠的企业，自购置符合条件的专用设备在5年内转让、出租的，应当停止享受企业所得税优惠，并补缴已经抵免的企业所得税税款。转让的受让方可以按照该专用设备投资额的10％抵免当年企业所得税应纳税额；当年应纳税额不足抵免的，可以在以后5个纳税年度结转抵免。选项C，甲企业转让设备可税前扣除的资产净值为固定资产计税基础（100万元）减去计提的折旧等之后的余额。选项D，甲企业转让设备时，按照规定计算缴纳增值税，不需要转出已抵扣的进项税额。<br>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>12.甲、乙两家企业是关联企业。2024年1月1日，乙企业从甲企业借款3 000万元，期限为一年，双方约定按照金融企业同类同期贷款年利率6％结算利息，乙企业无其他关联方债权性投资。乙企业注册资本为200万元，假设每月所有者权益构成均为实收资本200万元、资本公积100万元、未分配利润－50万元。2024年乙企业不得扣除的关联方借款利息为（　）万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.180<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.144<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.90<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.0<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255836_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255836_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255836_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255836_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255836_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255836_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255836_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255836_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』B<br>
『答案解析』实际支付的关联方利息＝3 000×6％＝180（万元）；关联债资比例＝年度各月平均关联债权投资之和÷年度各月平均权益投资之和＝（3 000×12）÷（300×12）＝10；不得扣除利息支出＝年度实际支付的全部关联方利息×（1－标准比例÷关联债资比例）＝180×（1－2÷10）＝144（万元）。<br>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>13.甲公司、乙公司、丙自然人成立了一个合伙企业，当年该合伙企业的生产经营所得和其他所得共计120万元。合伙协议中并未约定应纳税所得额的分配比例，甲公司、乙公司、丙自然人在协商确定分配比例时未能达成一致意见，已知甲公司实缴出资10万元，乙公司实缴出资20万元，丙自然人实缴出资30万元。那么该合伙企业合伙人甲公司当年应确定的应纳税所得额为（　）万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.20<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.30<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.40<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.60<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255837_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255837_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255837_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255837_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255837_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255837_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255837_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255837_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』A<br>
『答案解析』合伙企业的合伙人按照下列原则确定应纳税所得额：①合伙企业的合伙人以合伙企业的生产经营所得和其他所得，按照合伙协议约定的分配比例确定应纳税所得额；②合伙协议未约定或者约定不明确的，以全部生产经营所得和其他所得，按照合伙人协商决定的分配比例确定应纳税所得额；③协商不成的，以全部生产经营所得和其他所得，按照合伙人实缴出资比例确定应纳税所得额；④无法确定出资比例的,以全部生产经营所得和其他所得，按照合伙人数量平均计算每个合伙人的应纳税所得额。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>本题根据上述原则，合伙协议未约定且协商不成时，应按照合伙人实缴出资比例确定应纳税所得额。甲公司应确定的应纳税所得额＝120×10÷（10＋20＋30）＝20（万元）。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>14.关于企业政策性搬迁相关资产计税成本的确定，下列说法正确的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.企业搬迁过程中外购的固定资产，以购买价款和支付的相关税费作为计税成本<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.企业搬迁中被征用的土地，采取土地置换的，以换入土地的评估价值作为计税成本<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.企业简单安装即可继续使用的搬迁资产，以该项资产净值与安装费用合计数作为计税成本<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.企业需要大修理才能重新使用的搬迁资产，以该资产净值与大修理支出合计数作为计税成本<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255838_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255838_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255838_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255838_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255838_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255838_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255838_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255838_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』D<br>
『答案解析』选项A，企业搬迁过程中外购的固定资产，以购买价款和支付的相关税费以及直接归属于使该资产达到预定用途发生的其他支出为计税基础。选项B，企业搬迁中被征用的土地，采取土地置换的，换入土地的计税成本按被征用土地的净值，以及该换入土地投入使用前所发生的各项费用支出，为该换入土地的计税成本。选项C,企业搬迁的资产，简单安装或不需要安装即可继续使用的，在该资产重新投入使用后,就其净值按《企业所得税法》及其实施条例规定的该资产尚未折旧或摊销的年限，继续计提折旧或摊销。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>15.下列所得中，按“特许权使用费所得”缴纳个人所得税的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.编剧从任职单位取得的剧本使用费<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.退休后再任职取得的收入<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>16.贾某2025年3月因身体原因提前2年退休，企业按照统一标准发放给贾某一次性补贴150 000元。贾某应就该项一次性补贴缴纳的个人所得税为（　）元。<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.750<br>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>17.取得综合所得的居民个人，其发生符合扣除标准的下列支出中，只能在个人所得税汇算清缴时办理扣除的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.继续教育支出<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.个人养老金支出<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.子女教育支出<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.大病医疗支出<br>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>22.2025年4月曾女士作为人才被引进甲公司，该公司将购置价为660 000元的一套住房以330 000元的价格出售给曾女士。曾女士取得该住房应缴纳个人所得税（　）元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.64 590<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.78 490<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.73 995<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.79 840<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255846_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255846_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255846_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255846_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255846_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255846_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255846_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255846_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』D<br>
『答案解析』单位按低于购置或建造成本价格出售住房给职工，职工因此而少支出的差价部分，不并入当年综合所得，以差价收入除以12个月得到的数额，按照月度税率表确定适用税率和速算扣除数，单独计算纳税。计税公式为：应纳税额＝职工实际支付的购房价款低于该房屋的购置或建造成本价格的差额×适用税率－速算扣除数。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>（660 000－330 000）÷12＝27 500（元），适用税率为25％，速算扣除数为2 660元。应缴纳个人所得税＝（660 000－330 000）×25％－2 660＝79 840（元）。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>23.下列各项中，免征个人所得税的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.个人购买福利彩票，中奖5万元<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.个人达到国家规定的退休年龄，领取的企业年金<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.个人取得省级人民政府颁发的科技进步奖<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.退休人员再任职取得的收入<br>

『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』选项A，个人购买彩票的一次中奖收入，不超过1万元暂免征收个人所得税；超过1万元的，全额征收个人所得税。选项B，个人达到国家规定的退休年龄,领取的企业年金、职业年金，符合规定的，不并入综合所得，全额单独计算个人所得税应纳税款。选项D，按照“工资、薪金所得”计算个人所得税。<br>

</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255853_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255853_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255853_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255853_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255853_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255853_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255853_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255853_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』B<br>
『答案解析』采用引力法将扩大常设机构所在国的征税范围，有助于防止跨国纳税人利用国际税负差别进行避税。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</li></ul><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:23:39');" class="play-btn" title="点击跳到本段播放(00:23:39)"></a></div></div><div class="ask-box"><div class="commonAsk-wrap"><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="openAiFaqWithLecture('NODE04763100100100000130', '1001');" class="ask-btn" id="divask_NODE04763100100100000130" style="display: none;float:right; vertical-align:top; line-height:22px; font-size:12px; color:#fff; position:relative; font-weight:normal; padding:0 8px; background:#ffa443; border-radius:6px; text-decoration:none;">针对本讲义进行提问</a></div><div class="memoDiv" id="div_NODE04763100100100000130" ondblclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:24:09');" style="cursor:pointer;" title="双击跳到本段播放(00:24:09)"><ul><li style="word-break: break-all; font-size: 12px;">
<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>30.下列情形已经缴纳的印花税可以申请退还或者抵缴的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.应税合同、应税产权转移书据所列的金额与实际结算金额不一致，变更应税凭证后所列金额减少的<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.未履行的应税合同<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.未履行的产权转移书据<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.纳税人多贴的印花税票<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255854_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255854_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255854_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255854_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255854_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255854_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255854_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255854_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』A<br>
『答案解析』选项A，应税合同、应税产权转移书据所列的金额与实际结算金额不一致，不变更应税凭证所列金额的，以所列金额为计税依据；变更应税凭证所列金额的，以变更后的所列金额为计税依据。已缴纳印花税的应税凭证，变更后所列金额增加的，纳税人应当就增加部分的金额补缴印花税；变更后所列金额减少的，纳税人可以就减少部分的金额向税务机关申请退还或者抵缴印花税。选项B、C，未履行的应税合同、产权转移书据，已缴纳的印花税不予退还及抵缴税款。选项D，纳税人多贴的印花税票，不予退税及抵缴税款。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>31.基本养老保险基金涉及的下列投资业务中，免征印花税的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.养老基金将持有的证券，在养老基金证券账户之间的划拨过户<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.对社保基金会及养老基金投资管理机构运用养老基金买卖证券<br>

『正确答案』C<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>32.下列关于房产税纳税义务发生时间的说法，正确的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.纳税人出租房产，自交付房产之月起计征房产税<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.房地产开发企业自用本企业建造的商品房，自房屋使用之月起计征房产税<br>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>35.某房地产开发企业2024年10月通过政府拍卖受让一宗土地使用权，支付土地出让金7 000万元，取得合法票据。按照4％税率计算缴纳契税280万元，并取得完税凭证。2025年1月准备开工建设，因客观原因土地容积率被调低，财政部门通知可以退还土地出让金1 000万元。该房地产开发企业实际应缴纳契税（　）万元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.0<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.160<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.240<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.280<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255859_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255859_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255859_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255859_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255859_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255859_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255859_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255859_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』退还土地出让金时可以申请退还已缴纳的契税，实际应缴纳的契税＝（7 000－1 000）×4％＝240（万元）。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</li></ul><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:27:29');" class="play-btn" title="点击跳到本段播放(00:27:29)"></a></div></div><div class="ask-box"><div class="commonAsk-wrap"><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="openAiFaqWithLecture('NODE04763100100100000136', '1001');" class="ask-btn" id="divask_NODE04763100100100000136" style="display: none;float:right; vertical-align:top; line-height:22px; font-size:12px; color:#fff; position:relative; font-weight:normal; padding:0 8px; background:#ffa443; border-radius:6px; text-decoration:none;">针对本讲义进行提问</a></div><div class="memoDiv" id="div_NODE04763100100100000136" ondblclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:28:17');" style="cursor:pointer;" title="双击跳到本段播放(00:28:17)"><ul><li style="word-break: break-all; font-size: 12px;">
<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>36.单位或个人的下列经济行为，免征契税的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.个人购买面积为130平方米的家庭第二套住房<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.因共有人减少导致承受方增加房屋权属<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.个人承受经济适用住房房屋权属<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.作股投入本人独资经营企业的自有房产<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255860_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255860_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255860_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255860_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255860_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255860_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255860_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255860_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』D<br>
『答案解析』选项A，自2024年12月1日起，对个人购买家庭第二套住房，面积为140平方米及以下的，减按1％的税率征收契税；面积为140平方米以上的，减按2％的税率征收契税。选项B，承受方应依法缴纳契税。选项C，对个人购买经济适用住房，在法定税率基础上减半征收契税。选项D，同一投资主体内部所属企业之间土地、房屋权属的划转，包括母公司与其全资子公司之间，同一公司所属全资子公司之间，同一自然人与其设立的个人独资企业、一人有限公司之间土地、房屋权属的划转，免征契税。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</li></ul><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:28:17');" class="play-btn" title="点击跳到本段播放(00:28:17)"></a></div></div><div class="ask-box"><div class="commonAsk-wrap"><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="openAiFaqWithLecture('NODE04763100100100000137', '1001');" class="ask-btn" id="divask_NODE04763100100100000137" style="display: none;float:right; vertical-align:top; line-height:22px; font-size:12px; color:#fff; position:relative; font-weight:normal; padding:0 8px; background:#ffa443; border-radius:6px; text-decoration:none;">针对本讲义进行提问</a></div><div class="memoDiv" id="div_NODE04763100100100000137" ondblclick="cdelvideo.flashapi.seekVideo('00:28:45');" style="cursor:pointer;" title="双击跳到本段播放(00:28:45)"><ul><li style="word-break: break-all; font-size: 12px;">
<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>37.下列土地，免征城镇土地使用税的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.火电厂厂区围墙内的用地<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.港口的码头用地<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.纳税单位无偿使用免税单位的土地<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.矿山企业的办公用地<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255861_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255861_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255861_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255861_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255861_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255861_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255861_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255861_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』B<br>
『答案解析』选项B，对港口的码头（即泊位，包括岸边码头、伸入水中的浮码头、堤岸、堤坝、栈桥等）用地，免征城镇土地使用税；港口的其他用地，应按规定征收城镇土地使用税。选项A、C、D，按照规定计算缴纳城镇土地使用税。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>38.某市公园实际占用土地面积为10 000平方米，其中供公共参观游览用地2 800平方米，附设饮食部、照相馆用地各2 000平方米，公园管理单位办公用地3 200平方米。已知当地城镇土地使用税年税额为8元/平方米，则该公园每年应缴纳城镇土地使用税（　）元。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.32 000<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.16 000<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.40 000<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.12 000<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255862_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255862_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255862_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255862_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255862_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255862_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255862_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255862_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』A<br>
『答案解析』公园内供公共参观游览的用地及其管理单位的办公用地免征城镇土地使用税；公园中附设的营业场所，如影剧院、饮食部、茶社、照相馆等用地，应征收城镇土地使用税。该公园每年应缴纳城镇土地使用税＝（10 000－2 800－3 200）×8＝32 000（元）。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>39.下列各项中，按照当地适用税额减半征收耕地占用税的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.铁路线路占用耕地<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.医疗机构内职工住房占用耕地<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.农村居民在规定用地标准以内占用耕地新建自用住宅<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.军用观测台站占用耕地<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255863_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255863_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255863_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255863_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255863_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255863_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255863_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255863_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』C<br>
『答案解析』选项A，铁路线路占用耕地，减按每平方米2元的税额征收耕地占用税。选项B，医疗机构内职工住房占用耕地的，按照当地适用税额缴纳耕地占用税。选项C，农村居民在规定用地标准以内占用耕地新建自用住宅，按照当地适用税额减半征收耕地占用税，可以同时享受“六税两费” 减半优惠政策。选项D，军用观测台站占用耕地，免征耕地占用税。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<table class="tableA" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0"><tbody><tr><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;">
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>40.下列关于船舶吨税的说法，正确的是（　）。<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>A.拖船和机动驳船分别按相同净吨位船舶税率的50％计征税款<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>B.船舶吨税实行比例税率<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>C.船舶吨税纳税义务发生时间为应税船舶在港口停泊超过吨税执照期限的当日<br>
<span class="span_cdel_blank_sign"><span class="span_cdel_blank_sign" contenteditable="false">　　</span></span>D.船舶吨税由海关负责征收<br>
</td></tr><tr id="tr_show_6255864_1" class="picShow class_tr_show_6255864_1" style="display: block;"><td colspan="3" style="font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer01.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showAnswer('6255864_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_hide_6255864_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255864_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtHideTd" colspan="3" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer04.gif&quot;); font-size: 12px;"><img src="http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer02.gif" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="hideAnswer('6255864_1');"></td></tr><tr id="tr_answer_6255864_1" class="jyTxt class_tr_6255864_1" style="display:none;"><td class="jyTxtAnswerTd" style="background-image: url(&quot;http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/cwresources/chinaacc/images/kanke/m_answer03.gif&quot;); background-repeat: repeat-y; width: 16px; font-size: 12px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" style="text-align: left; width: 98%; font-size: 12px;">
『正确答案』D<br>
『答案解析』选项A，拖船和非机动驳船分别按相同净吨位船舶税率的50％计征税款。选项B，船舶吨税设置普通税率和优惠税率，均为定额税率。选项C，船舶吨税纳税义务发生时间为应税船舶进入港口的当日。<br>
</td></tr></tbody></table>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var handleQuestionClick= function(jyID, videoID,status) {
        var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        var dyForumID = pageData.dyForumID;
        var cwID = pageData.cwID;
        var homeSubjectID = pageData.homeSubjectID;
        if (status == null || status == "") {
            status = 2;
        }
        if (status == 2) {//未报课，跳转到免费答疑页面
            var url = "//member.chinaacc.com/faq/free/lecture/query.shtm?Forum_ID=" + dyForumID + "&qclass=b0015&QNo=" + jyID + "&cwareID=" + cwareID;
            url += "&Jy_url=[KCJYGET," + cwareID + "," + videoID + "," + jyID + ",ISNEW]";
            url += "&identity=" + homeSubjectID;
            window.open(url);
        } else {
            var url = "//member.chinaacc.com/faq/interface/faqView.shtm?cwID=" + cwID + "&qclass=b0015&QNo=" + jyID;
            url += "&Jy_url=[KCJYGET," + cwareID + "," + videoID + "," + jyID + ",ISNEW]";
            url += "&identity=" + homeSubjectID;
            window.open(url);
        }
    }

    function openAiFaqWithLecture(jyID, videoID) {
        const aiFaqMenuItem = document.getElementById('click_aiFaq');
        if (!aiFaqMenuItem) return;

        // 1. 展开“提问”面板
        if (!$(aiFaqMenuItem).hasClass('on')) {
            $(aiFaqMenuItem).trigger('click');
        }

        // 2. 准备参数
        const cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
        const cwID = pageData.cwID;
        const subjectId = pageData.cwareSubjectID;
        const majorID = pageData.cwareEduID;

        const faqUrl = "https://member.chinaacc.com/aiFaq/miniFaq?" +
            $.param({
                topicID: null,
                majorID: majorID,
                subjectId: subjectId,
                cwID: cwID,
                cwareID: cwareID,
                videoID: videoID,
                jyID: jyID,
                isLive: 0
            });

        // 3. 更新 iframe 的 src（即使已加载也刷新，确保内容更新）
        const $frame = $("#aiFaqFrame");
        $frame.attr("src", faqUrl).data("loaded", true);
    }
</script>

	var csPop = function (el,nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID) {
		var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
		var videoID = pageData.videoID;
        $.getJSON(pageData.basePath+'/testPop/getPointFlag.shtm',{
            cwareID:cwareID,
            videoID:videoID,
            r:Math.random()
        },function(data){
			// 控制div显示（0 都不显示设置选项，1 都显示显示，2 显示知识点测试，3 显示单元测试）
			var test = data[0];
			console.log(test);
			// 两个设置选项
			var setPointTest = $('#setPointTest');
			var setUnitTest = $('#setUnitTest');
			switch (test.settingFlag) {
				case 1:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				case 2:
					setPointTest.show();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
				case 3:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.show();
					break;
				default:
					setPointTest.hide();
					setUnitTest.hide();
					break;
			}
            $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
            $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
			$("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");

            for (var i = 0, len = data.length; i < len; i++) {
                var test = data[i];
                var currOpenType = test.pointOpenType;
                switch (currOpenType) {
                    case "z": //知识点测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"zPopFlag0":"zPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
                    case "d": //单元测试
                        var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"dPopFlag0":"dPopFlag1"
                        $("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
                        break;
					case "t": //知识点练习
						var chickID = test.pointFlag == 0?"tPopFlag0":"tPopFlag1"
						$("#"+chickID).addClass("on").siblings('li').removeClass('on');
						break;
                    default :
                        $("#zPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#dPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        $("#tPopFlag1").addClass("on");
                        break;
                }
            }

        });
		var _this = $("." + el);
		var myHeight = _this.height();
		_this.css("marginTop", -myHeight / 2)
		$(".mask").show();
		_this.show();
	}

<script>

    function clearEditImgData() {
        $(".screenshot-note-dialog").hide();
        $(".screenshot-note-dialog-mask").hide();
        $("#editImgContent").val('');
        $('.note-num span').text(0);
        // 清除img
        $("#editResult").attr('src', '');
        $("#videoRefID").val('');
        $("#editImg .note-img ul li").remove();
        $('#editImg .note-img span').html(0);
        // 恢复截图提交按钮
        $(".screenshot-note-container .note-mod .note-fotter .note-btn.submit-btn").prop('disabled', false);
        window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
    }

<script src="/xcware/cwresources/js/lib/require.js?bust=2.1.13.9" data-main="/xcware/cwresources/js/main/h5video/h5VideoPlayApp20190813.js?bust=2.1.13.9">

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
	var tpjb = false;
	if (tpjb) {
		var tpjbtime=window.setInterval(function(){ 
			if (window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getMediaStatus() == "play"
				&& $(".menu .pjqp .pop").css('display') == 'none') {
					$(".menu .pjqp .pop").stop(true,true).fadeIn();
					var tpjbtimeout=window.setTimeout(function(){
						$(".menu .pjqp .pop").stop(true,true).fadeOut();
						window.clearTimeout(tpjbtime);
					}, 1000 * 4);
				}
		}, 1000 * 1);

	}
	
	//var refreshuserid=window.setInterval(function(){ 
	//	refreshsid();
	//}, 1000 * 60 * 30);
	$("#click_lecture").one('click', function() {
    // 使用 setTimeout 延时 200ms 执行
    setTimeout(function() {
        // 补丁：点击讲义时定位到当前讲义位置
        window.jyView.selectLecture(window.jyView.getCurrJyID());
    }, 300); // 200 毫秒延时
});
	
	
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var isTy = $("#isTy").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
    
    if(isTy == '1' && statusCode == '2'){
    	var videoLen = $("#videoLen").val();
    	var showFlag = true;
    	var completeTimer=window.setInterval(function(){ 
    		var time = window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getNowPlayingTime();
    		if(Math.abs(videoLen - time) < 4 && showFlag){
    			showFlag = false;
    			completePlay();
    		}
    	}, 1000 * 1);
	}

    
	if(statusCode == '1' && isTy =='0' && tjcwareID != '' && tjvideoID != ''){
		var teacherHideTime = new Date().getTime();//上次隐藏老师时间
		var pauseTime = new Date().getTime();//上次暂停时间
		var speedTime = new Date().getTime();//上次超过一倍速播放时间
		var openTimeLine = 1000 * 60 * 5;//5分钟弹出
		var openTimeLinePause = 1000 * 3;//暂停3秒弹出
		
		var pointLen = $("#pointLen").val();
		var pointArr = pointLen.split(',');
		var playPointNum = 0;
		var playSeekNum = 0;
		var nowPlayTime = 0;
		var videoShowUpdate = window.setInterval(function(){ 
			var openTip = $("#openTip").val();//0弹框 1不弹
			//暂停触发being
			var now = new Date().getTime();
			if (window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getMediaStatus() == "pause"){
				if(now - pauseTime > openTimeLinePause && openTip == '0'){
					openTip = '1';
					courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-experience');
				}
			}
			if (window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getMediaStatus() == "play"){
				pauseTime = new Date().getTime();
			}
			//暂停触发end
			//隐藏老师触发begin
			if(window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getIsHideTeacher() == '1'){//隐藏
				if(openTip == '0' && now - teacherHideTime > openTimeLine){
					//alert('隐藏老师弹出');
					openTip = '1';
					var tyData = $("#tyData").val();
					courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
				}
			}else{//未隐藏
				teacherHideTime = new Date().getTime();
			}
			//隐藏老师触发end
			
			//倍速触发begin
			 if(window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getCurrentSpeed() > 1){//隐藏
				if(openTip == '0' && now - speedTime > openTimeLine){
					openTip = '1';
					courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
				}
			}else{//未隐藏
				speedTime = new Date().getTime();
			} 
			//倍速触发
			//学习时间
			var time = window.cdelvideo.flashapi.getNowPlayingTime();
			
			if(openTip == '0'){
				if(time - nowPlayTime > 5 && nowPlayTime > 0){
					playSeekNum ++;
					if(playSeekNum > 1){
						openTip = '1';
						courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
					}
				}
			}
			nowPlayTime = time;
			$("#openTip").val(openTip);
		}, 1000 * 1);
	}
// 	TODO 初始化页面 需要加载观看人数
	initStydyNums();
});
// 初始化学习人数
function initStydyNums() {
	var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
	var videoID = pageData.videoID;
	postAesData({
		data: {
			params: {
				"cwareID": cwareID,
				"videoID": videoID
			},
			domain: "chinaacc",
			resourcePath: "+/innercware/service/getCwareVisitCount",
			af: "1",
			ap: "pc"
		},
		// ajax成功回调
		success: function (data) {
			if (data.success) {
				if (data.result.show == 1) {
					$(".stydyNums").text(data.result.countForPaid + "人已学习");
				}
			}
		}
	});
}
function courseUpgradePrompt(id) {
    var _main = $('.'+ id);
    _main.show().css('margin-left',-(_main.width()/2));
    //退出全屏
    if(document.exitFullscreen) {
        document.exitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.mozCancelFullScreen) {
        document.mozCancelFullScreen();
    } else if(document.webkitExitFullscreen) {
        document.webkitExitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.msExitFullscreen) {
        document.msExitFullscreen();
    }
}

function showTjVideo(id, dm,category, context){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var experienceProductId = $("#openProductId").val();
	var lowShiftsProductId = $("#lowShiftsProductId").val();
	var subject =  $("#subject").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
    track(dm, category, context);
	if(statusCode == '1'){//有体验资格没有升级资格
		$.getJSON("http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/openClass.shtm?experienceProductId="+experienceProductId+"&lowShiftsProductId="+lowShiftsProductId,
		  	     function(data){
		  		   if(data.success != undefined && data.success){//开课成功
		  			 window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		  			 //closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		  			 var url = 'http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/videoPlay.shtm?cwareID='+tjcwareID+'&videoID='+tjvideoID;
		  			 window.open(url,"_blank");
		  		  }else{
		  			 window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		  			 //closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		  			 alert('开通体验课失败');
		  		  }
		});
	}else{
		window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		//closeCourseUpgrade(id);
		var url = 'http://elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/h5video/videoPlay.shtm?cwareID='+tjcwareID+'&videoID='+tjvideoID;
		window.open(url,"_blank");
	}
}

function courseUpgrade(id) {
    var _main = $('.'+ id);
    _main.parents('.courseUpgrade-mod').show();
    _main.show().css('margin-top',-(_main.height()/2)).siblings('.courseUpgrade-main').hide();
    if(document.exitFullscreen) {
        document.exitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.mozCancelFullScreen) {
        document.mozCancelFullScreen();
    } else if(document.webkitExitFullscreen) {
        document.webkitExitFullscreen();
    } else if(document.msExitFullscreen) {
        document.msExitFullscreen();
    }
}
//closeCourseUpgrade(id,callback)  id 关闭弹窗的id  callbackId 弹出确认弹窗id
function closeCourseUpgrade(id,callbackId, dm, category, context){
    var _main = $('.'+ id);
    _main.hide().css('margin-top',0).parents('.courseUpgrade-mod').hide();
    if(callbackId && callbackId != ''){
        courseUpgrade(callbackId)
    }
    track(dm, category, context);
}

function completePlay(){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var isTy = $("#isTy").val();
	if(statusCode == '2' && isTy == '1'){
		window.cdelvideo.flashapi.pauseVideo();
		courseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-upgrade');
	}
}

function playNext(dm, category, context){
	window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
	closeCourseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-upgrade');
	track(dm, category, context);
}

function updateClass(dm, category, context){
	var upgradeClassID = $("#upgradeClassID").val();
	var details = $("#details").val();
	var url = 'http://sale.chinaacc.com/newweb/upgrade/upgradeInfo.shtm?viewClassId=' + upgradeClassID + '&detailIds=' + details;
	window.open(url,"_blank");
	closeCourseUpgrade('courseUpgrade-upgrade');
	track(dm, category, context);
}

function askktty_result(id){
	closeCourseUpgrade(id);
	var url=basePath+"/faqNew/faqAsk.shtm";
	var jyID = $("#jyID").val();
	var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val();
	var videoID = $("#videoID").val();
	var title = $("#title").val();
	var content = $("#askContent").val();
	var Jy_url="[KCJYGET,"+cwareID+","+videoID+","+jyID+",ISNEW]";
	$.post(url, {
		cwareID: cwareID,
		qclass: '100b',
		QNo: jyID,
		Jy_url: Jy_url,
		title: title,
		content: content
	},function(data){ 
		var result = eval("(" + data + ")");
		if(result["flag"] == true){$("#title").val("");
			$("#askContent").val("");
			window.faqvideoPlay._winAlert("提示信息","提问成功,您可以在播放器下方的答疑区查看您的提问!");
			window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
			//显示提问信息
			window.faqvideoPlay.faqAllAsk(1);
			//关闭窗口
			window.newpage._closeItem(window.newpage);
		}else{
			$("#title").val("");
			$("#askContent").val("");
			window.faqvideoPlay._winAlert("错误信息",result["msg"]);
			window.cdelvideo.flashapi.playVideo();
			//关闭窗口
			window.newpage._closeItem(window.newpage);
		}
		// 剩余文字初始化
		$("#askContent").trigger("propertychange");
		$("#askContent").trigger("input");
	});
}

function pointTest(){
	var statusCode = $("#statusCode").val();
	var isTy = $("#isTy").val();
	var tjcwareID = $("#tjcwareID").val();
    var tjvideoID = $("#tjvideoID").val();
	var openTip = $("#openTip").val();
	var playPointNum = $("#playPointNum").val();
	playPointNum++;
	if(openTip == '0' && playPointNum > 2 && (statusCode == '1'||statusCode == '2') && isTy =='0' && tjcwareID != '' && tjvideoID != ''){
		courseUpgradePrompt('courseUpgrade-prompt');
		$("#openTip").val('1');
	}
	$("#playPointNum").val(playPointNum);
}


function track(dm, category, context) {
	if(category != undefined && context != undefined && dm != undefined){
		CDELTracker.$track(dm, {
			"category" : category,
			"context" : context
		});
	}
}

//判断sid是否有效，无效时进行踢出登录
function refreshsid(){
	$.getJSON("//elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/video/userSession/refresh.shtm",
	  	 function(data){ 
		   if(data.code != undefined && data.code == -1){//登录状态失效 
			   window.location.href = "//elearning.chinaacc.com/xcware/error.jsp?userFlag=3";
	  		}
	});
}

// 触发埋点功能方法
function buried(dm) {
	var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val(); // 课件编号
	var videoID = $("#videoID").val(); // 视频编号
	var cwareEduID = $("#cwareEduID").val(); // 辅导id
	var subject = $("#subject").val(); // 科目id
	CDELTracker.$track(dm, {
		"$custom_cwareID" : cwareID,
		"$custom_videoID" : videoID,
		"$custom_cwareEduID" : cwareEduID,
		"$custom_cwareSubjectID" : subject
	});
}

$('.eyeColorBox ul li').click(function (){
	var smallColorClass = $(this).attr('data-color');
	$(this).parents('eyeMode').find('a').removeClass(smallColorClass);
	$(this).addClass('on').siblings('li').removeClass('on');
	$('.eyeHoverBtn').removeClass('changeBlue changeYellow changeGreen').addClass(smallColorClass);
	$('.splitsWrap ,#lecture').removeClass('changeBlue changeYellow changeGreen').addClass(smallColorClass);
	setCookies("eyeModeIndex",$(this).index());
	setCookies("eyeModeColor",smallColorClass);
})


function setCookies(name,value)
{
	var Days = 1;
	var exp  = new Date();
	exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + Days*30*60*1000);
	document.cookie = name + "="+ escape(value) +";domain=chinaacc.com;path=/;";
}


function getCookie2(name){
	var strcookie = document.cookie;//获取cookie字符串
	var arrcookie = strcookie.split("; ");//分割
	//遍历匹配
	for ( var i = 0; i < arrcookie.length; i++) {
		var arr = arrcookie[i].split("=");
		if (arr[0] == name){
			return arr[1];
		}
	}
	return "";
}

//写个方法判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
function setIsScaleScroll(){
	window.isScaleScroll = true;
	clearTimeout($.data(this, 'scaleTimer'));
	$.data(this, 'scaleTimer', setTimeout(function() {
		window.isScaleScroll = false;
	}, 500));
}

		//字体切换 //字体放大缩小
$(".setFontNormal a").click(function () {
	var _type = $(this)[0].id;
	var bl = $(".lectureCon .memoDiv b,.memoDiv .showIsAnswer");
	var allItem = $(".lectureCon li,td");
	//ai智能看逐字稿
	let aiTranscriptDiv = $("#aiTranscript");
	switch (_type) {
		case 'bigger':
			var fontSize = [];
			for (var i = 0; i < allItem.length; i++) {
				var _item = $(allItem[i]);
				var _size = parseInt(_item.css("font-size").split("px")[0])
				//console.log(_size)
				_item.css({"font-size": (_size + 1) + "px"});
				bl.css({"font-size": (_size + 1) + "px"})
				fontSize.push(_size + 1);
			}
			setUserFontSize(fontSize);
			if($(".font14zd") && $(".font14zd").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".font14zd").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".font14zd").css({"font-size": (redSize + 1) + "px"});
			}
			if($(".fontKaiti") && $(".fontKaiti").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".fontKaiti").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".fontKaiti").css({"font-size": (redSize + 1) + "px"});
			}
			//ai智能看逐字稿
			if(aiTranscriptDiv.length > 0){
				let aiFontSize = parseInt(aiTranscriptDiv.css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				aiTranscriptDiv.css({"font-size": (aiFontSize + 1) + "px"});
			}
			//判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
			setIsScaleScroll();
			break;
		case 'normal':
			allItem.css({"font-size": "14px"});
			var allItemTd = $(".lectureCon td");
			allItemTd.css({"font-size": "12px"});
			setUserFontSize([16,12]);
			bl.css({"font-size": "14px"});
			$(".lectureCon .font14").css({"font-size": "14px"});
			$(".lectureCon .font16").css({"font-size": "16px"});
			if($(".font14zd") && $(".font14zd").css("font-size")){
				$(".font14zd").css({"font-size": "14px"});
			}
			if($(".font16zd")){
				$(".font16zd").css({"font-size": "16px"});
			}
			if($(".fontKaiti")){
				$(".fontKaiti").css({"font-size": "15px"});
			}
			//ai智能看逐字稿
			if(aiTranscriptDiv.length > 0){
				aiTranscriptDiv.css({"font-size": "14px"});
			}
			//判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
			setIsScaleScroll();
			break;
		case 'smaller':
			if (allItem.css("font-size") == "10px") {
				return;
			}
			var fontSize = [];
			for (var i = 0; i < allItem.length; i++) {
				var _item = $(allItem[i]);
				var _size = parseInt(_item.css("font-size").split("px")[0])
				_item.css({"font-size": (_size - 1) + "px"});
				bl.css({"font-size": (_size - 1) + "px"});
				fontSize.push(_size - 1);
			}
			setUserFontSize(fontSize);
			if($(".font14zd") && $(".font14zd").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".font14zd").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".font14zd").css({"font-size": (redSize - 1) + "px"});
			}
			if($(".fontKaiti") && $(".fontKaiti").css("font-size")){
				var redSize = parseInt($(".fontKaiti").css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				$(".fontKaiti").css({"font-size": (redSize - 1) + "px"});
			}
			//ai智能看逐字稿
			if(aiTranscriptDiv.length > 0){
				let aiFontSize = parseInt(aiTranscriptDiv.css("font-size").split("px")[0]);
				aiTranscriptDiv.css({"font-size": (aiFontSize - 1) + "px"});
			}
			//判断是否缩放导致的滚动条位置变化
			setIsScaleScroll();
			break;
	}

})

var myNotePop = function (el,nodeID,userID,pictureUrls) {
	$("#nodeID").val(nodeID);
	$("#userID").val(userID);
	var _this = $("." + el);
	var myHeight = _this.height();
	_this.css("marginTop", -myHeight / 2)
	$(".mask").show();
	_this.show();
	if (el === "notesModify") {
		var _textarea = $(".textAreaBox textarea" )
		_textarea.val("");
		_textarea.val($("#modify_" + nodeID).text());
		$(".textAreaBox i").text(_textarea.val().toString().trim().length+'/800');
		console.log(pictureUrls)
		var pic = pictureUrls.split(",");
		$(".notesModify .picBox-more").show();
		$(".notesModify #pic-list").html("")
		for(var j=0;j<pic.length;j++){
			if (pic[j]!=''){
				$(".notesModify #pic-list").append("<a href=\"javascript:void(0)\" class=\"picBox-img\"><span onclick=\"myNotePicPop('"+pic[j]+"')\"><img src=\""+pic[j]+"\"></span><i class=\"close\"></i></a>");
			}
		}
		$(".notesModify .picBox-img .close").on('click', function() {
			$(this).parent(".picBox-img").remove();
			if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length<3&&$(".notesModify .picBox-more").is(":hidden")){
				$(".notesModify .picBox-more").show();
			}
			$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
		})
		if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length>=3){
			$(".notesModify .picBox-more").hide();
		}
		$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
	}
}

	//var myHeight = _this.height();

	$(".mask-pic").show();
	_this.show();
	//_this.find(".pic").css("margin-top", - _this.find(".pic").height() / 2);
	//_this.find(".pic").css("margin-left", - _this.find(".pic").width() / 2);
}

var mindMapPreview = function (url) {
	url = url.replace("_chg","");

	_this.css("background-color", "white");//加上白色背景防止思维导图黑色字体看不见

	_this.css("height", "500px");
	_this.find(".pic").attr("src",url);
	_this.find(".pic").css("max-width", "900px");
	_this.find(".pic").css("max-height", "500px");

	_this.show();
}

	$("."+el).hide();
	if (el == 'amplifyPicPop') {
		$(".mask-pic").hide();
	}else{
		$(".mask").hide();
	}
	if (el ==="deleteNote" &&  e ==="1"){
		$(".deleteBox").hide();
		var nodeID = $("#nodeID").val();
		var userID = $("#userID").val();
		var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val();
		noteDel(nodeID,userID,cwareID);
	}

}
var modifyUploadFile = function () {
	$("#modifyUploadFile").click();
}
$("#modifyUploadFile").on("change",function (e) {
	var e = e
	//获取 文件 个数 取消的时候使用
	var files = e.target.files;
	if(files.length>0){
		for(var i=0;i<files.length;i++){
			//调用上传图片方法
			modifyUploadImg(files[i]);
		}
	}
});
var modifyUploadImg = function (file) {
	var time = this.toDateTimeStr2(new Date());
	$.get(pageData.basePath+"/upload/getMd5Code.shtm?str="+time+"&cwareID="+pageData.cwareID,function(data){
		if(data === ""){
			alert("上传错误")
		}else{
			var fd = new FormData();
			fd.append("files",file);
			fd.append('origin', "CWARE");
			fd.append('time', time);
			fd.append("securecode", data);
			$.ajax({
				url: pageData.basePath+"/upload/image.shtm?cwareID="+pageData.cwareID,
				type: 'POST',
				async: false,
				contentType: false,
				processData: false,
				dataType: 'json',
				data: fd,
				success: function(data){
					if(data.code==0){
						// alert("图片上传成功!");
						$(".notesModify #pic-list").append("<a href=\"javascript:void(0)\" class=\"picBox-img\"><span onclick=\"myNotePicPop('"+data.imageUrl+"')\"><img src=\""+data.imageUrl+"\"></span><i class=\"close\"></i></a>");
						if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length==3){
							$(".notesModify .picBox-more").hide();
						}
						$(".notesModify .picBox-img .close").on('click', function() {
							console.log(2222)
							$(this).parent(".picBox-img").remove();
							if ($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length<3&&$(".notesModify .picBox-more").is(":hidden")){
								$(".notesModify .picBox-more").show();
							}
							$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
						})
						$('.notesModify .picBox-num em').html($(".notesModify #pic-list").children("a").length);
					}else{
						alert(data.msg);
					}
				},
			});
		}
	})
}

function toDateTimeStr2(intTime){
	var date;
	if(intTime == null){
		date = new Date();
	}else{
		date = new Date(intTime);
	}
	var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
	if(month < 10){
		month = "0" + month;
	}
	var day = date.getDate();
	if(day < 10){
		day = "0" + day;
	}
	var hours = date.getHours();
	if(hours < 10){
		hours = "0" + hours;
	}
	var m = date.getMinutes();
	if(m < 10){
		m = "0" + m;
	}
	var s = date.getSeconds();
	if(s < 10){
		s = "0" + s;
	}
	return date.getFullYear() + "-" + month + "-" + day + " " + hours + ":" + m + ":" + s;
};

var noteDel  = function(nodeID,userID,cwareID){
	var basePath = pageData.basePath;
	/*if(!confirm("您确定要删除该条笔记吗?")) {
		return false;
	}*/
	$.post(basePath+"/viewNode/load/delViewNote.shtm", {
		nodeID : nodeID,
		userID : userID,
		cwareID : cwareID,
		r:Math.random()
	},function(data){
		var result = eval("(" + data + ")");
		if(result >0){
			alert("删除成功!");
			init();
		}else{
			alert("删除失败！");
		}
	});
}
$(".textAreaBox textarea").bind('input propertychange',function (){
	let trim =  $(".textAreaBox textarea").val().trim();
	var textAreaBox_i = $(".textAreaBox i")
	if (trim.toString().length>800){
		textAreaBox_i.css("color","red");
	}else{
		textAreaBox_i.css("color","#999");
	}
	textAreaBox_i.text(trim.toString().length+'/800');
})
var submitNote = function () {
	closeMyNotePop("notesModify","0")
	var nodeID = $("#nodeID").val();
	var userID = $("#userID").val();
	var cwareID = $("#cwareID").val();
	var videoID = $("#videoID").val();
	var picStr = "";
	if ($(".notesModify .picBox-img span img").length>0){
		for (var i = 0;i<$(".notesModify .picBox-img span img").length;i++){
			if (i==($(".notesModify .picBox-img span img").length-1)){
				picStr = picStr + $(".notesModify .picBox-img span img")[i].src;
			}else {
				picStr = picStr + $(".notesModify .picBox-img span img")[i].src+",";
			}
		}
	}
	noteUpdateSubmit(nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID,picStr);

}
//笔记修改保存
var  noteUpdateSubmit = function(nodeID,userID,cwareID,videoID,pictureUrls){
	var basePath = pageData.basePath;
	var nodeContent = $(".textAreaBox textarea" ).val();
	if(nodeContent.length>800){
		alert("内容过长，最多输入800字 ！");
		return;
	}
	$.post(basePath+"/viewNode/load/addViewNote.shtm", {
		nodeID:nodeID,
		cwareID:cwareID,
		videoID:videoID,
		nodeContent:nodeContent,
		pictureUrls:pictureUrls,
		r:Math.random()

	}, function(data) {
		var result = eval("(" + data + ")");
		if(result >0){
			alert("保存成功！");
			init();

		}else{
			alert("保存失败！");
		}
	});
}

//初始化加载方法
var init = function(){
	//初始化显示当前视频笔记
	var basePath = pageData.basePath;
	var statPath = pageData.statPath;
	var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
	var videoID = pageData.videoID;
	var iconUrl = pageData.iconUrl;
	var tableStr = "";
	$.getJSON(basePath+"/viewNode/load/getAllNoteList.shtm",{
		cwareID:cwareID,
		videoID:videoID,
		r:Math.random()
	},function(data){
		var obj = data;
		var dataLen = obj.length;
		if(dataLen>0){
			tableStr += "<ul>";
			for(var i=0;i<dataLen;i++){
				tableStr += "<li><span id='modify_"+obj[i].nodeID+"'>"+obj[i].nodeContent+"</span>" ;
				var s = "<p class=\"noteConList\">"+"<span class='noteTime'>"+(obj[i].updateTime)+"</span>";
				s+= '<span style="margin-top: -25px;" class="buttonFunction fr">\n' +
						'<a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="jumpVideo('+"'"+obj[i].nodeID+"'"+')" class="fontC"><i class="noteIcon icon01" ></i>收听相关课程</a>' +
						'<a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="myNotePop(\'notesModify\','+"'"+obj[i].nodeID+"',"+"'"+obj[i].userID+"',"+"'"+obj[i].pictureUrls+"'"+')" class="fontC"><i class="noteIcon icon02" ></i>修改</a>' +
						'<a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="myNotePop(\'deleteBox\','+"'"+obj[i].nodeID+"',"+"'"+obj[i].userID+"'"+')" class="fontC"><i class="noteIcon icon03" ></i>删除</a>' +
						'</span>';
				var reg = new RegExp("\n","g");
				tableStr +=s.replace(reg,"<br/>");
                tableStr +="</p>";
                if (obj[i].pictureUrls){
                    tableStr +="<div class='picBox clearfix'>";
                    var pic = obj[i].pictureUrls.split(",")
                    for(var j=0;j<pic.length;j++){
                        if (pic[j]!=''){
                            // pic[j] = "https://img.cdeledu.com/CWARE/2022/0111/561a3b15ff74ef66-0.png";
                            tableStr +="<a href='javascript:void(0)' class='picBox-img' onclick=\"window.note.myNotePicPop('"+pic[j]+"')\"><img src='"+pic[j]+"'></a>";
                        }
                    }
                    tableStr +="</div>";
                }
				tableStr +=" </li>";
			}
			tableStr +="</ul>";
		}else{
			tableStr +="<div class='tip tip_null'></div>";
		}
		$("#noteWrap").html(tableStr);
	});
}


function setUserFontSize(size){//设置用户字体大小的cookie
	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate()+60);
	document.cookie="userVideoLectureFontSize=" +escape(size)+ "; path=/xcware/" +";expires="+exdate.toGMTString();
}

//设置是否显示AI智能看的cookie（1为显示AI看，0为显示讲义，默认为0）
function setIsShowAiCookie(val){
	setCookies("isShowAiLook", val);
}
//获取是否显示AI智能看的cookie
function getIsShowAiCookie(){
	let isAiLook = 0;//默认显示讲义
	let isAiLookCookie = getCookie2("isShowAiLook");
	if (isAiLookCookie){
		isAiLook = isAiLookCookie;
	}
	return isAiLook;
}

//AI智能看、思维导图、同步讲义、全部讲义等按钮切换
function tabClick(divId){
	switch (divId){
		case "aizhinengkan":
			//ai看
			$("#toolsDiv").show();
			$("#lectureDiv").hide();
			$("#contentDiv").show();
			$("#aiTranscript").show();
			$("#mindMap").hide();
			$("#allLecture").hide();
			setIsShowAiCookie(1);
			break;
		case "siweidaotu":
			//思维导图
			$("#toolsDiv").hide();
			$("#aiTranscript").hide();
			$("#mindMap").show();
			$("#allLecture").hide();
			setIsShowAiCookie(0);
			break;
			//全部讲义
		case "quanbujiangi":
			$("#toolsDiv").show();
			$("#lectureDiv").show();
			$("#contentDiv").hide();
			$("#aiTranscript").hide();
			$("#mindMap").hide();
			$("#allLecture").show();
			setIsShowAiCookie(0);
			break;
		default:
			break;
	}
}
//AI智能看内容定位功能点击事件
$(".aiLocateMode a").click(function () {
	$(this).toggleClass("on");
	if($(this).hasClass("on")){
		//开启内容定位
		window.isScrollAi = true;
	}else{
		//关闭内容定位
		window.isScrollAi = false;
	}
});

$("#tryout .title .close").click(function () {
	$("#courseBox").stop(true).animate({right: "-360px"}, 200);
	$("#courseBox").removeClass("courseShow");
	$(".menu .menuCur").removeClass();
	$(".menu a.menuBack").remove();
	//$(".section").hide();
})
$(".set-tryout-box .set-con ul li").click(function () {
	$(this).addClass('on').siblings('li').removeClass('on')
})

function testFlag(flag, type) {
	window.testController.closePoint4Click();
	if(type == 'z') {
		pageData.pointZFlag = flag;
	}
	if(type == 'd') {
		pageData.pointDFlag = flag;
	}
	if(type == 't') {
		pageData.pointTFlag = flag;
	}
	var cwareID = pageData.cwareID;
	var videoID = pageData.videoID;
	var innerCwareID = pageData.innerCwareID;
	$.getJSON(pageData.basePath+'/testPop/updatePointFlag.shtm',{
		pointOpenType:type,
		pointFlag:flag,
		cwareID:cwareID,
		videoID:videoID,
		innerCwareID:innerCwareID,
		r:Math.random()
	},function(data){
		console.log(data)
	});
}

}
